import Deliverable\nfrom .mutation_inventory import MutationInventoryResult\nfrom .state_detector import DetectionResult\n\n\nclass NodeOperation(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Operation type for a data flow 'D-0015' -> 'M0015').\"\"\"\n        import re\n        m = re.match(r\"D(\\d+)\\.\", self.deliverable_id)\n        if m:\n            return f\"M{m.group(1)}\"\n        m = re.match(r\"D-(\\d+)\", self.deliverable_id)\n        if m:\n            return f\"M{m.group(1)}\"\n        return f\"M-{self.deliverable_id}\"\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass DataFlowEdge:\n    \"\"\"A directed edge from a write/birth node to a read node.\n\n    Attributes:\n        source: The write/birth node.\n        target: The read node.\n        is_cross_milestone: True if source and target are in different milestones.\n        source_milestone: Milestone of the source node.\n        target_milestone: Milestone of the target node.\n    \"\"\"\n    source: DataFlowNode\n    target: DataFlowNode\n    is_cross_milestone: bool = False\n    source_milestone: str = \"\"\n    target_milestone: str = \"\"\n\n    def __post_init__(self) -> None:\n        if not self.source_milestone:\n            self.source_milestone = self.source.milestone\n        if not self.target_milestone:\n            self.target_milestone = self.target.milestone\n        if not self.is_cross_milestone:\n            self.is_cross_milestone = self.source_milestone != self.target_milestone\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass DataFlowGraph:\n    \"\"\"Directed graph tracing state variables through deliverables.\n\n    Uses adjacency list representation for O(V+E) operations.\n    \"\"\"\n    nodes: list[DataFlowNode] = field(default_factory=list)\n    edges: list[DataFlowEdge] = field(default_factory=list)\n add_node(self, node: DataFlowNode) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Add a node to the graph.\"\"\"\n        if node not in self._node_set:\n            self.nodes.append(node)\n            self._node_set.add(node)\n            self._adjacency.setdefault(node, [])\n\n    def add_edge(self, edge: DataFlowEdge) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Add a directed edge to the graph.\"\"\"\n        self.add_node(edge.source)\n        self.add_node(edge.target)\n        self.edges.append(edge)\n        self._adjacency[edge.source].append(edge)\n\n    @property\n    def cross_milestone_edges(self) -> list[DataFlowEdge]:\n        \"\"\"All edges that cross milestone boundaries.\"\"\"\n        return [e for e in self.edges if e.is_cross_milestone]\n\n    def outgoing(self, node: DataFlowNode) -> list[DataFlowEdge]:\n        \"\"\"Get outgoing edges from a node.\"\"\"\n        return self._adjacency.get(node, [])\n\n    def detect_cycles(self) -> list[list[DataFlowNode]]:\n        \"\"\"Detect cycles using iterative DFS with coloring.\n\n        Returns list of cycles found (each cycle is a list of nodes).\n        \"\"\"\n        WHITE, GRAY, BLACK = 0, 1, 2\n        color: dict[DataFlowNode, int] = {n: WHITE for n in self.nodes}\n        parent: dict[DataFlowNode, DataFlowNode | None] = {}\n        cycles: list[list[DataFlowNode]] = []\n\n        for start in {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-opus-4-6","id":"msg_01NpCr2rAGMpwsWoBcpEKYUg","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01MUp6AyscBfr5WVaRiudAoa","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/contract_extractor.py","content":"\"\"\"Implicit contract extractor -- extracts cross-milestone contracts from data flow edges.\n\nFor each cross-milestone edge in the data flow graph, parses:\n- Writer semantics: \"set X to mean Y\", \"X represents Z after this operation\"\n- Reader assumptions: \"assumes X is\", \"when X equals\", \"based on X\"\n\nBelow 60% confidence -> UNSPECIFIED with mandatory human review flag.\n\nR-013 acknowledged: implicit contract extraction from natural language has\nfundamental reliability limits. UNSPECIFIED below 60% with mandatory human\nreview is the mitigation.\n\nNFR-007: No imports from superclaude.cli.sprint or superclaude.cli.roadmap.\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport re\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field\n\nfrom .dataflow_graph import DataFlowEdge, DataFlowGraph\nfrom .models import Deliverable\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Data structures\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nUNSPECIFIED = \"UNSPECIFIED\"\nCONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD = 0.60\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass ImplicitContract:\n    \"\"\"A contract between a writer and reader across milestone boundaries.\n\n    Attributes:\n        variable: Name of the state variable.\n        writer_deliverable: ID of the deliverable performing the write.\n        reader_deliverable: ID of the deliverable performing the read.\n        writer_semantics: What the writer claims the variable means after writing.\n        reader_assumption: What the reader assumes the variable means.\n        writer_confidence: Confidence score for writer semantics extraction (0.0-1.0).\n        reader_confidence: Confidence score for reader assumption extraction (0.0-1.0).\n        needs_human_review: True if either confidence < CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD.\n    \"\"\"\n    variable: str\n    writer_deliverable: str\n    reader_deliverable: str\n    writer_semantics: str = UNSPECIFIED\n    reader_assumption: str = UNSPECIFIED\n    writer_confidence: float = 0.0\n    reader_confidence: float = 0.0\n\n    @property\n    def needs_human_review(self) -> bool:\n        return (\n            self.writer_confidence < CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD\n            or self.reader_confidence < CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD\n        )\n\n    @property\n    def overall_confidence(self) -> float:\n        \"\"\"Combined confidence (geometric mean of writer and reader).\"\"\"\n        return (self.writer_confidence * self.reader_confidence) ** 0.5\n\n    @property\n    def is_fully_specified(self) -> bool:\n        return (\n            self.writer_semantics != UNSPECIFIED\n            and self.reader_assumption != UNSPECIFIED\n        )\n\n    @property\n    def highest_risk(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Both sides UNSPECIFIED -> highest risk.\"\"\"\n        return (\n            self.writer_semantics == UNSPECIFIED\n            and self.reader_assumption == UNSPECIFIED\n        )\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Writer semantic patterns\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n_WRITER_PATTERNS: list[tuple[re.Pattern, float]] = [\n    # \"set X to mean Y\" / \"set X to represent Y\"\n    (re.compile(r\"\\bset\\s+\\w+\\s+to\\s+(?:mean|represent|indicate|track)\\s+(.+?)(?:\\.|,|$)\", re.IGNORECASE), 0.85),\n    # \"X represents Y after this\"\n    (re.compile(r\"\\b\\w+\\s+represents?\\s+(.+?)(?:\\.|,|$)\", re.IGNORECASE), 0.80),\n    # \"X tracks Y\" / \"X counts Y\"\n    (re.compile(r\"\\b\\w+\\s+(?:tracks?|counts?|measures?|records?)\\s+(.+?)(?:\\.|,|$)\", re.IGNORECASE), 0.80),\n    # \"store Y in X\" / \"write Y to X\"\n    (re.compile(r\"\\b(?:store|write|save|persist)\\s+(.+?)\\s+(?:in|to|into)\\s+\\w+\", re.IGNORECASE), 0.75),\n    # \"X equals Y after\" / \"X will be Y\"\n    (re.compile(r\"\\b\\w+\\s+(?:equals?|will\\s+be|becomes?|is\\s+set\\s+to)\\s+(.+?)(?:\\.|,|$)\", re.IGNORECASE), 0.75),\n    # \"update X with Y\" / \"update X to Y\"\n    (re.compile(r\"\\bupdate\\s+\\w+\\s+(?:with|to)\\s+(.+?)(?:\\.|,|$)\", re.IGNORECASE), 0.70),\n    # \"increment X by Y\" / \"advance X by Y\"\n    (re.compile(r\"\\b(?:increment|advance|increase|decrease)\\s+\\w+\\s+by\\s+(.+?)(?:\\.|,|$)\", re.IGNORECASE), 0.75),\n    # Weaker: \"X is Y\"\n    (re.compile(r\"\\b\\w+\\s+is\\s+(?:the\\s+)?(.+?)(?:\\.|,|$)\", re.IGNORECASE), 0.55),\n]\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Reader assumption patterns\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n_READER_PATTERNS: list[tuple[re.Pattern, float]] = [\n    # \"assumes X is Y\" / \"assumes X equals Y\"\n    (re.compile(r\"\\bassumes?\\s+\\w+\\s+(?:is|equals?|contains?|represents?)\\s+(.+?)(?:\\.|,|$)\", re.IGNORECASE), 0.90),\n    # \"when X equals Y\" / \"when X is Y\"\n    (re.compile(r\"\\bwhen\\s+\\w+\\s+(?:equals?|is|reaches?|exceeds?)\\s+(.+?)(?:\\.|,|$)\", re.IGNORECASE), 0.85),\n    # \"based on X\" / \"depends on X\"\n    (re.compile(r\"\\b(?:based\\s+on|depends?\\s+on|relies?\\s+on)\\s+(.+?)(?:\\.|,|$)\", re.IGNORECASE), 0.70),\n    # \"expects X to be Y\"\n    (re.compile(r\"\\bexpects?\\s+\\w+\\s+to\\s+(?:be|equal|contain|represent)\\s+(.+?)(?:\\.|,|$)\", re.IGNORECASE), 0.85),\n    # \"if X then\" / \"check if X\"\n    (re.compile(r\"\\b(?:if|check\\s+(?:if|whether))\\s+\\w+\\s+(?:is|equals?|has|contains?)\\s+(.+?)(?:\\s+then|\\.|,|$)\", re.IGNORECASE), 0.75),\n    # \"X should be Y\" / \"X must be Y\"\n    (re.compile(r\"\\b\\w+\\s+(?:should|must|shall)\\s+(?:be|equal|contain)\\s+(.+?)(?:\\.|,|$)\", re.IGNORECASE), 0.80),\n    # \"requires X\" / \"needs X\"\n    (re.compile(r\"\\b(?:requires?|needs?)\\s+(.+?)(?:\\.|,|$)\", re.IGNORECASE), 0.60),\n    # Weaker: \"uses X\" / \"reads X\"\n    (re.compile(r\"\\b(?:uses?|reads?|accesses?|fetches?)\\s+(.+?)(?:\\.|,|$)\", re.IGNORECASE), 0.50),\n]\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Extraction\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\ndef extract_writer_semantics(\n    description: str, variable_name: str,\n) -> tuple[str, float]:\n    \"\"\"Extract writer semantics from a deliverable description.\n\n    Returns (semantics_text, confidence). Returns (UNSPECIFIED, 0.0)\n    if no pattern matches or confidence < threshold.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not description:\n        return UNSPECIFIED, 0.0\n\n    best_match: str = UNSPECIFIED\n    best_confidence: float = 0.0\n\n    for pattern, base_confidence in _WRITER_PATTERNS:\n        for m in pattern.finditer(description):\n            extracted = m.group(1).strip()\n            if not extracted:\n                continue\n\n            # Boost confidence if variable name is near the match\n            var_lower = variable_name.lower().lstrip(\"_\")\n            proximity_boost = 0.05 if var_lower in description.lower()[max(0, m.start()-50):m.end()+50] else 0.0\n            confidence = min(base_confidence + proximity_boost, 1.0)\n\n            if confidence > best_confidence:\n                best_confidence = confidence\n                best_match = extracted\n\n    if best_confidence < CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD:\n        return UNSPECIFIED, best_confidence\n\n    return best_match, best_confidence\n\n\ndef extract_reader_assumption(\n    description: str, variable_name: str,\n) -> tuple[str, float]:\n    \"\"\"Extract reader assumption from a deliverable description.\n\n    Returns (assumption_text, confidence). Returns (UNSPECIFIED, 0.0)\n    if no pattern matches or confidence < threshold.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not description:\n        return UNSPECIFIED, 0.0\n\n    best_match: str = UNSPECIFIED\n    best_confidence: float = 0.0\n\n    for pattern, base_confidence in _READER_PATTERNS:\n        for m in pattern.finditer(description):\n            extracted = m.group(1).strip()\n            if not captured, got UNSPECIFIED (conf={r_conf})\"\n        assert w_conf >= CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD\n        assert r_conf >= CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD\n\n    def test_full_contract_extraction(self):\n        \"\"\"Full pipeline: graph -> cross-milestone edge -> contract extracted.\"\"\"\n        graph = DataFlowGraph()\n        writer = DataFlowNode(\"D1.1\", \"offset\", NodeOperation.WRITE)\n Direct contradiction: writer and reader state opposite things\n2. Scope mismatch: filtered subset vs full set\n3. Type mismatch: boolean vs integer, etc.\n4. Completeness mismatch: partial vs complete\n\nCross-references M2 invariant predicates and failure mode tables.\nExtensible synonym dictionary (R-014 mitigation).\n\nNFR-007: No imports from superclaude.cli.sprint or superclaude.cli.roadmap.\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport re\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field\nfrom enum import Enum\n\nfrom .contract_extractor import UNSPECIFIED, ImplicitContract\nfrom .invariants import InvariantEntry\n\n\nclass ConflictKind(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Classification of conflict type.\"\"\"\n    DIRECT_CONTRADICTION = \"direct_contradiction\"\n    SCOPE_MISMATCH = \"scope_mismatch\"\n    TYPE_MISMATCH = \"type_mismatch\"\n    COMPLETENESS_MISMATCH = \"completeness_mismatch\"\n    UNSPECIFIED_WRITER = \"unspecified_writer\"\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass ConflictDetection:\n    \"\"\"A detected conflict between writer semantics and reader assumptions.\n\n    Attributes:\n        contract: The ImplicitContract containing the conflict.\n        kind: Classification of the conflict.\n        description: Human-readable description of the divergence.\n        suggested_resolution: Recommended action to resolve.\n        severity: \"high\" | \"medium\" | \"low\" based on conflict kind.\n    \"\"\"\n    contract: ImplicitContract\n    kind: ConflictKind\n    description: str\n    suggested_resolution: str\n    severity: str = \"medium\"\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Extensible synonym dictionary (R-014 mitigation)\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nSYNONYM_GROUPS: list[set[str]] = [\n    {\"total\", \"count\", \"number\", \"quantity\", \"sum\", \"amount\"},\n    {\"all\", \"every\", \"complete\", \"full\", \"entire\", \"whole\"},\n    {\"filtered\", \"subset\", \"partial\", \"selected\", \"matching\", \"qualifying\"},\n    {\"processed\", \"handled\", \"completed\", \"finished\", \"consumed\", \"delivered\"},\n    {\"offset\", \"position\", \"index\", \"cursor\", \"pointer\", \"location\"},\n    {\"flag\", \"boolean\", \"bool\", \"toggle\", \"switch\", \"indicator\"},\n    {\"integer\", \"int\", \"number\", \"numeric\", \"count\"},\n    {\"string\", \"str\", \"text\", \"name\", \"label\"},\n    {\"active\", \"enabled\", \"on\", \"true\", \"running\"},\n    {\"inactive\", \"disabled\", \"off\", \"false\", \"stopped\"},\n]\n\n# Build lookup: word -> set of synonyms\n_SYNONYM_LOOKUP: dict[str, set[str]] = {}\nfor group in SYNONYM_GROUPS:\n    for word in group:\n        _SYNONYM_LOOKUP[word] = group\n\n\ndef are_synonyms(word1: str, word2: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if two words are synonyms according to the dictionary.\"\"\"\n    w1 = word1.lower().strip()\n    w2 = word2.lower().strip()\n    if w1 == w2:\n        return True\n    group = _SYNONYM_LOOKUP.get(w1, set())\n    return w2 in group\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Scope indicators\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n_SCOPE_ALL = {\"all\", \"every\", \"complete\", \"full\", \"entire\", \"total\", \"whole\"}\n_SCOPE_FILTERED = {\"filtered\", \"subset\", \"partial\", \"selected\", \"matching\", \"some\", \"qualifying\"}\n\n# Type indicators\n_TYPE_BOOLEAN = {\"boolean\", \"bool\", \"flag\", \"true\", \"false\", \"toggle\"}\n_TYPE_INTEGER = {\"integer\", \"int\", \"number\", \"count\", \"numeric\", \"counter\"}\n_TYPE_STRING = {\"string\", \"str\", \"text\", \"name\"}\n_TYPE_GROUPS = [_TYPE_BOOLEAN, _TYPE_INTEGER, _TYPE_STRING]\n\n# Contradiction indicators\n_POSITIVE_INDICATORS = {\"delivered\", \"processed\", \"completed\", \"sent\", \"written\", \"all\", \"total\"}\n_NEGATIVE_INDICATORS = {\"undelivered\", \"unprocessed\", \"pending\", \"remaining\", \"failed\", \"none\"}\n\n\ndef _tokenize(text: str) -> set[str]:\n    \"\"\"Tokenize text into lowercase words.\"\"\"\n    return set(re.findall(r\"\\b\\w+\\b\", text.lower()))\n\n\ndef _detect_scope_mismatch(writer_tokens: set[str], reader_tokens: set[str]) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Detect scope mismatch: one side says 'all/total', other says 'filtered/subset'.\"\"\"\n    writer_has_all = bool(writer_tokens & _SCOPE_ALL)\n    writer_has_filtered = bool(writer_tokens & _SCOPE_FILTERED)\n    reader_has_all = bool(reader_tokens & _SCOPE_ALL)\n    reader_has_filtered = bool(reader_tokens & _SCOPE_FILTERED)\n\n    return (writer_has_all and reader_has_filtered) or (writer_has_filtered and reader_has_all)\n\n\ndef _detect_type_mismatch(writer_tokens: set[str], reader_tokens: set[str]) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Detect type mismatch: writer implies one type, reader implies another.\"\"\"\n    for i, group_a in enumerate(_TYPE_GROUPS):\n        for group_b in _TYPE_GROUPS[i + 1:]:\n            writer_in_a = bool(writer_tokens & group_a)\n            reader_in_b = bool(reader_tokens & group_b)\n            writer_in_b = bool(writer_tokens & group_b)\n            reader_in_a = bool(reader_tokens & group_a)\n            if (writer_in_a and reader_in_b) or (writer_in_b and reader_in_a):\n                return True\n    return False\n\n\ndef _detect_direct_contradiction(writer_tokens: set[str], reader_tokens: set[str]) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Detect direct contradiction: writer says positive, reader says negative or vice versa.\"\"\"\n    writer_pos = bool(writer_tokens & _POSITIVE_INDICATORS)\n    writer_neg = bool(writer_tokens & _NEGATIVE_INDICATORS)\n    reader_pos = bool(reader_tokens & _POSITIVE_INDICATORS)\n    reader_neg = bool(reader_tokens & _NEGATIVE_INDICATORS)\n\n    return (writer_pos and reader_neg) or (writer_neg and reader_pos)\n\n\ndef _detect_completeness_mismatch(\n    writer_tokens: set[str],\n    reader_tokens: set[str],\n    invariant_entry: InvariantEntry | None = None,\n) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Detect completeness mismatch using semantic and invariant cross-reference.\"\"\"\n    # Check for partial vs complete indicators\n    completeness_full = {\"complete\", \"all\", \"total\", \"full\", \"entire\"}\n    completeness_partial = {\"partial\", \"some\", \"subset\", \"incremental\", \"batch\"}\n\n    writer_full = bool(writer_tokens & completeness_full)\n    writer_partial = bool(writer_tokens & completeness_partial)\n    reader_full = bool(reader_tokens & completeness_full)\n    reader_partial = bool(reader_tokens & completeness_partial)\n\n    if (writer_full and reader_partial) or (writer_partial and reader_full):\n        return True\n\n    # Cross-reference with invariant entry for enriched detection\n    if invariant_entry:\n        pred_tokens = _tokenize(invariant_entry.invariant_predicate)\n        if pred_tokens & completeness_full and reader_partial:\n            return True\n\n    return False\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Main detector\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\ndef detect_conflicts(\n    contracts: list[ImplicitContract],\n    invariant_entries: list[InvariantEntry] | None = None,\n    fmea_severity_map: dict[str, str] | None = None,\n) -> list[ConflictDetection]:\n    \"\"\"Detect conflicts in implicit contracts.\n\n    Args:\n        contracts: List of ImplicitContract from T04.02.\n        invariant_entries: M2 invariant entries for cross-reference enrichment.\n        fmea_severity_map: M2 FMEA severity map for completeness enrichment.\n\n    Returns:\n        List of ConflictDetection objects.\n    \"\"\"\n    if invariant_entries is None:\n        invariant_entries = []\n    if fmea_severity_map is None:\n        fmea_severity_map = {}\n\n    # Build invariant lookup\n    inv_lookup: dict[str, InvariantEntry] = {}\n    for entry in invariant_entries:\n        inv_lookup[entry.variable_name] = entry\n\n    conflicts: list[ConflictDetection] = []\n\n    for contract in contracts:\n        # Rule: UNSPECIFIED writer always conflicts (cannot verify compatibility)\n        if contract.writer_semantics == UNSPECIFIED:\n            conflicts.append(ConflictDetection(\n                contract=contract,\n                kind=ConflictKind.UNSPECIFIED_WRITER,\n                description=(\n                    f\"Writer semantics for '{contract.variable}' are UNSPECIFIED \"\n                    f\"in {contract.writer_deliverable}. Cannot verify compatibility \"\n                    f\"with reader {contract.reader_deliverable}.\"\n                ),\n                suggested_resolution=(\n                    f\"Add explicit semantic declaration for '{contract.variable}' \"\n                    f\"in deliverable {contract.writer_deliverable}.\"\n                ),\n                severity=\"high\",\n            ))\n            continue\n\n        # Skip if reader is also unspecified (already flagged via needs_human_review)\n        if contract.reader_assumption == UNSPECIFIED:\n            conflicts.append(ConflictDetection(\n                contract=contract,\n                kind=ConflictKind.UNSPECIFIED_WRITER,\n                description=(\n                    f\"Reader assumption for '{contract.variable}' is UNSPECIFIED \"\n                    f\"in {contract.reader_deliverable}.\"\n                ),\n                suggested_resolution=(\n                    f\"Add explicit assumption for '{contract.variable}' \"\n                    f\"in deliverable {contract.reader_deliverable}.\"\n                ),\n                severity=\"high\",\n            ))\n            continue\n\n        writer_tokens = _tokenize(contract.writer_semantics)\n        reader_tokens = _tokenize(contract.reader_assumption)\n        inv_entry = inv_lookup.get(contract.variable)\n\n        # Check each conflict type (in order of severity)\n        if _detect_direct_contradiction(writer_tokens, reader_tokens):\n            conflicts.append(ConflictDetection(\n                contract=contract,\n                kind=ConflictKind.DIRECT_CONTRADICTION,\n                description=(\n                    f\"Direct contradiction for '{contract.variable}': \"\n                    f\"writer says '{contract.writer_semantics}', \"\n                    f\"reader assumes '{contract.reader_assumption}'.\"\n                ),\n                suggested_resolution=(\n                    f\"Align writer and reader on the semantic meaning of \"\n                    f\"'{contract.variable}' across milestones.\"\n                ),\n                severity=\"high\",\n            ))\n        elif _detect_scope_mismatch(writer_tokens, reader_tokens):\n            conflicts.append(ConflictDetection(\n                contract=contract,\n                kind=ConflictKind.SCOPE_MISMATCH,\n                description=(\n                    f\"Scope mismatch for '{contract.variable}': \"\n                    f\"writer says '{contract.writer_semantics}', \"\n                    f\"reader assumes '{contract.reader_assumption}'.\"\n                ),\n                suggested_resolution=(\n                    f\"Clarify whether '{contract.variable}' represents a \"\n                    f\"filtered subset or the complete set.\"\n                ),\n                severity=\"high\",\n            ))\n        elif _detect_type_mismatch(writer_tokens, reader_tokens):\n            conflicts.append(ConflictDetection(\n                contract=contract,\n                kind=ConflictKind.TYPE_MISMATCH,\n                description=(\n                    f\"Type mismatch for '{contract.variable}': \"\n                    f\"writer implies '{contract.writer_semantics}', \"\n                    f\"reader assumes '{contract.reader_assumption}'.\"\n                ),\n                suggested_resolution=(\n                    f\"Standardize the type of '{contract.variable}' \"\n                    f\"across writer and reader deliverables.\"\n                ),\n                severity=\"medium\",\n            ))\n        elif _detect_completeness_mismatch(writer_tokens, reader_tokens, inv_entry):\n            conflicts.append(ConflictDetection(\n                contract=contract,\n                kind=ConflictKind.COMPLETENESS_MISMATCH,\n                description=(\n                    f\"Completeness mismatch for '{contract.variable}': \"\n                    f\"writer says '{contract.writer_semantics}', \"\n                    f\"reader assumes '{contract.reader_assumption}'.\"\n indicators\n_TYPE_BOOLEAN = {\"boolean\", \"bool\", \"flag\", \"true\", \"false\", \"toggle\"}\n_TYPE_INTEGER = {\"integer\", \"int\", \"number\", \"count\", \"numeric\", \"counter\"}\n_TYPE_STRING = {\"string\", \"str\", \"text\", \"name\"}\n_TYPE_GROUPS = [_TYPE_BOOLEAN, _TYPE_INTEGER, _TYPE_STRING]\n\n# Contradiction indicators\n_POSITIVE_INDICATORS = {\"delivered\", \"processed\", bool(writer_tokens & _SCOPE_FILTERED)\n    reader_has_all = bool(reader_tokens & _SCOPE_ALL)\n    reader_has_filtered = bool(reader_tokens & _SCOPE_FILTERED)\n\n    return (writer_has_all and reader_has_filtered) or (writer_has_filtered and reader_has_all)\n\n\ndef _detect_type_mismatch(writer_tokens: set[str], reader_tokens: set[str]) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Detect type mismatch: writer implies one type, reader implies another.\"\"\"\n    for i, group_a in enumerate(_TYPE_GROUPS):\n        for group_b in _TYPE_GROUPS[i + 1:]:\n            writer_in_a = bool(writer_tokens & group_a)\n            reader_in_b = bool(reader_tokens & group_b)\n            writer_in_b = bool(writer_tokens & group_b)\n            reader_in_a = bool(reader_tokens & group_a)\n            if (writer_in_a and reader_in_b) or (writer_in_b and reader_in_a):\n                return True\n    return False\n\n\ndef _detect_direct_contradiction(writer_tokens: set[str], reader_tokens: set[str]) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Detect direct contradiction: writer says positive, reader says negative or vice versa.\"\"\"\n    writer_pos = bool(writer_tokens & _POSITIVE_INDICATORS)\n    writer_neg = bool(writer_tokens & _NEGATIVE_INDICATORS)\n    reader_pos = bool(reader_tokens & _POSITIVE_INDICATORS)\n    reader_neg = bool(reader_tokens & _NEGATIVE_INDICATORS)\n\n    return (writer_pos and reader_neg) or (writer_neg and reader_pos)\n\n\ndef _detect_completeness_mismatch(\n    writer_tokens: set[str],\n    reader_tokens: set[str],\n    invariant_entry: InvariantEntry | None = None,\n) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Detect completeness mismatch using semantic and invariant cross-reference.\"\"\"\n    # Check for partial vs complete indicators\n    completeness_full = {\"complete\", \"all\", \"total\", \"full\", \"entire\"}\n    completeness_partial = {\"partial\", \"some\", \"subset\", \"incremental\", \"batch\"}\n\n    writer_full = bool(writer_tokens & completeness_full)\n    writer_partial = bool(writer_tokens & completeness_partial)\n    reader_full = bool(reader_tokens & completeness_full)\n    reader_partial = bool(reader_tokens & completeness_partial)\n\n    if (writer_full and reader_partial) or (writer_partial and reader_full):\n        return True\n\n    # Cross-reference with invariant entry for enriched detection\n    if invariant_entry:\n        pred_tokens = Cycles\n    cycles = graph.detect_cycles()\n    if cycles:\n        lines.append(f\"**Cycles detected**: {len(cycles)}\")\n        lines.append(\"\")\n\n    # Dead writes\n    dead_writes = graph.find_dead_writes()\n    if dead_writes:\n        lines.append(f\"**Dead writes**: {len(dead_writes)}\")\n        for dw in dead_writes:\n            lines.append(f\"  - `{dw.variable_name}` in `{dw.deliverable_id}`\")\n        lines.append(\"\")\n\n    #
